# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

## Context

- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)

- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

Perfect! I've created a comprehensive answer that documents all the Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the log segment and index architecture. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Components Identified:

**Core Architecture:**
- **LogSegment** - The main class encapsulating a single log segment with its log file and indices
- **OffsetIndex** - Sparse index mapping offsets to file positions (8-byte entries)
- **TimeIndex** - Maps timestamps to offsets for time-based queries (12-byte entries)
- **AbstractIndex** - Base class providing memory-mapped file management and binary search
- **TransactionIndex** - Tracks aborted transactions

**Configuration & File Management:**
- **LogConfig** - Defines all log-level configuration and validation
- **LogFileUtils** - Utilities for standard log and index file naming
- **FileRecords** - Abstraction for log file I/O with memory mapping

**Recovery on Startup:**
- **LogLoader** - Orchestrates log recovery with `recoverLog()` method processing unflushed segments
- **UnifiedLog** - Manages complete topic partition logs with local and remote segments
- **LocalLog** - Manages locally stored segments
- **LeaderEpochFileCache** - Caches leader epoch for offset tracking during recovery
- **LogManager** - Broker-wide log management with checkpoint coordination

**Checkpoint Files:**
- **OffsetCheckpointFile** - Persists recovery points and log start offsets
- **LeaderEpochCheckpointFile** - Maintains leader epoch information
- **CleanShutdownFileHandler** - Manages clean shutdown markers

**Supporting Components:**
- **LogSegments** - Thread-safe container for multiple segments
- **ProducerStateManager** - Tracks producer state for deduplication
- **RemoteIndexCache** - Caches remote index files for tiered storage
- **Clea

It manages the actual log data file (FileRecords) and three types of indices: OffsetIndex, TimeIndex, and TransactionIndex. The LogSegment class provides methods for appending records, recovering from failure, and managing the lifecycle of indices.\\n\\n## Index File Formats\\n\\n### OffsetIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/OffsetIndex.java)\\nImplements a sparse index mapping offsets to physical positions in the log file. Uses an 8-byte entry size with 4 bytes for offset and 4 bytes for position. Extends AbstractIndex with specialized binary search capabilities for offset lookup.\\n\\n### TimeIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TimeIndex.java)\\nMaintains a mapping of timestamps to offsets with a 12-byte entry size (8 bytes timestamp, 4 bytes relative offset). Critical for time-based log retention and timestamp-based message lookup.\\n\\n### AbstractIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/AbstractIndex.java)\\nBase class for index implementations providing memory-mapped file management, binary search, and index validation logic. Handles the underlying file I/O and memory mapping for efficient random access.\\n\\n### TransactionIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java)\\nTracks aborted transactions for consumer offset validation and idempotent producer deduplication.\\n\\n## Lazy Index Loading\\nLazyIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java) wraps index instances with deferred loading to defer memory mapping until first access, improving startup performance.\\n\\n## Configuration and Validation\\nLogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java) defines all log-level configuration properties and validation rules. The recoverLog() method processes unflushed segments above the recovery point checkpoint, rebuilding indices and validating consistency. It uses recovery checkpoints to avoid replaying the entire log.\\n\\n### UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java)\\nRepresents a complete topic partition log combining local and remote segments. Manages the overall log state and coordinates with LogLoader for recovery.\\n\\n### LocalLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java)\\nManages the local portion of a log with segments stored on the broker.\\n\\n## Checkpoint Files\\n\\n### OffsetCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpointFile.java)\\nPersists recovery point offsets and log start offsets to avoid full log recovery on clean shutdown. segment and index architecture is comprehensively implemented across multiple Java and Scala files in the apache/kafka repository. The core architecture consists of several key components:\\n\\n## Core Log Segment Class\\nThe LogSegment class (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java) is the central component that encapsulates a single log segment. It manages the actual log data file (FileRecords) and three types of indices: OffsetIndex, TimeIndex, and TransactionIndex. The LogSegment class provides methods for appending records, recovering from failure, and managing the lifecycle of indices.\\n\\n## Index File Formats\\n\\n### OffsetIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/OffsetIndex.java)\\nImplements a sparse index mapping offsets to physical positions in the log file. Uses an 8-byte entry size with 4 bytes for offset and 4 bytes for position. Extends AbstractIndex with specialized binary search capabilities for offset lookup.\\n\\n### TimeIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TimeIndex.java)\\nMaintains a mapping of timestamps to offsets with a 12-byte entry size (8 bytes timestamp, 4 bytes relative offset). Critical for time-based log retention and timestamp-based message lookup.\\n\\n### AbstractIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/AbstractIndex.java)\\nBase class for index implementations providing memory-mapped file management, binary search, and index validation logic. Handles the underlying file I/O and memory mapping for efficient random access.\\n\\n### TransactionIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java)\\nTracks aborted transactions for consumer offset validation and idempotent producer deduplication.\\n\\n## Lazy Index Loading\\nLazyIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java) wraps index instances with deferred loading to defer memory mapping until first access, improving startup performance.\\n\\n## Configuration and Validation\\nLogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java) defines all log-level configuration properties and validation rules. LogFileUtils (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogFileUtils.java) provides utilities for constructing standard log file and index file paths.\\n\\n## Log Recovery on Startup\\n\\n### LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java)\\nThe primary class orchestrating log recovery on startup. The recoverLog() method processes unflushed segments above the recovery point checkpoint, rebuilding indices and validating consistency. It uses recovery checkpoints to avoid replaying the entire log.\\n\\n### UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java)\\nRepresents a complete topic partition log combining local and remote segments. Manages the overall log state and coordinates with LogLoader for recovery.\\n\\n### LocalLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java)\\nManages the local portion of a log with segments stored on the broker.\\n\\n## Checkpoint Files\\n\\n### OffsetCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpointFile.java)\\nPersists recovery point offsets and log start offsets to avoid full log recovery on clean shutdown. The recovery-point-offset-checkpoint and log-start-offset-checkpoint files in each log directory track these offsets.\\n\\n### LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java)\\nMaintains leader epoch information for handling log truncation and replica divergence detection. Used in conjunction with LeaderEpochFileCache for epoch-based offset lookup.\\n\\n### CleanShutdownFileHandler (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/CleanShutdownFileHandler.java)\\nManages the clean shutdown marker file that signals whether recovery is needed.\\n\\n## Log Recovery Coordination\\n\\n### LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java)\\nCaches leader epoch entries and coordinates epoch-based offset queries during recovery and replication.\\n\\n### LogManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/log/LogManager.scala)\\nManages all log instances for a broker. The checkpointLogRecoveryOffsets() method periodically writes recovery point checkpoints to enable fast startup recovery.\\n\\n### LogSegments (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegments.java)\\nThread-safe container for managing multiple LogSegment instances with navigation and range query capabilities.\\n\\n## Supporting Components\\n\\n### FileRecords (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/record/FileRecords.java)\\nAbstraction over raw log file I/O with memory mapping support for efficient record reading.\\n\\n### ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java)\\nTracks producer state for idempotent and transactional message deduplication, recovered during log recovery.\\n\\n### RemoteIndexCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/RemoteIndexCache.java)\\nCaches remote index files for tiered storage, integrating with the main index architecture.\\n\\n### Cleaner (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/Cleaner.java)\\nManages log compaction, accessing indices for retention decisions.\\n\\nThe architecture ensures reliable message persistence, fast recovery from failures, and efficient message lookup through a sophisticated system of sparse indices, checkpoint files, and recovery mechanisms.\"\n}\n",
